namespace = agot_nicknames

#Generic Nicknames
agot_nicknames.0100 = {
	type = character_event
	hidden = yes

	#Makes them important
	trigger = {
		has_any_nickname = no
		is_adult = yes
		OR = {
			prestige >= 500
			is_ruler = yes
			any_close_family_member = {
				is_ruler = yes
			}
			has_trait = kingsguard
			has_trait = education_martial_prowess_3
			has_trait = education_martial_prowess_4
			has_trait = education_martial_prowess_5
		}
	}
	option = {
		random_list = {
			1000 = {

			}
			50 = { #Heroic Nicknames
				trigger = {
					prowess >= 25
					ai_boldness >= medium_positive_boldness
				}
				random_list = {
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_agot_the_warrior }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_agot_greysteel }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_agot_fireball }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_agot_hardstone }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_agot_breakspear }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_agot_oakenfist }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_agot_greatheart }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_agot_ironheart }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_agot_the_neveryield }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_agot_greycloak }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_agot_longspear }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_agot_shieldbreaker }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_agot_shieldsmasher }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_agot_thunderbolt }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_agot_the_steelskin }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_agot_the_woe }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_agot_the_morningstar }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_agot_oakenshield }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_agot_blacksword }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_agot_widowmaker }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_agot_bloodborn }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_agot_starfire }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_agot_the_windrider }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_agot_swiftspur }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_agot_battleborn }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_agot_swordbiter }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_agot_the_painter }
				}
			}
			50 = { #Monstrous Nicknames
				trigger = {
					OR = {
						martial >= 14
						prowess >= 20
					}
					OR = {
						has_trait = strong
						has_trait = physique_good
						has_trait = giant
						has_trait = athletic
					}
					OR = {
						has_trait = sadistic
						has_trait = callous
						has_trait = wrathful
						has_trait = impatient
						has_trait = vengeful
						has_trait = beauty_bad #misunderstood cause they ugly :(
					}
				}
				random_list = {
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_agot_the_awful }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_agot_the_brute }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_agot_the_beast }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_agot_hard }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_agot_the_butcher }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_agot_the_demon }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_agot_the_monster_large }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_agot_the_slaughterer }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_agot_the_fiend }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_agot_the_gargoyle }
				}
			}
			50 = { #Good Martial
				trigger = {
					martial >= 20
				}
				random_list = {
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_agot_the_anvil }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_agot_the_tactician }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_agot_the_trebuchet }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_agot_the_warlord }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_agot_the_battlemaster }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_agot_the_stone }
				}
			}
			50 = { #Good Diplo
				trigger = {
					diplomacy >= 18
					NOT = { has_trait = callous }
					NOT = { has_trait = rude }
					NOT = { has_trait = wrathful }
				}
				random_list = {
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_agot_silvertongue }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_agot_the_affable }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_agot_the_jovial }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_agot_the_jolly }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_agot_the_merry }

				}
			}
			50 = { #Good Learning
				trigger = {
					learning >= 18
				}
				random_list = {
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_agot_the_reader }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_agot_the_learned }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_agot_the_scholar }

					1 = { give_nickname = nick_agot_the_lettered }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_agot_the_erudite }
				}
			}
			50 = { #Good Intrigue
				trigger = {
					intrigue >= 18
				}
				random_list = {
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_agot_the_shadow }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_agot_the_dagger }

					1 = { give_nickname = nick_agot_pennylover }
				}
			}
			50 = { #Attractive Men
				trigger = {
					is_female = no
					has_trait = beauty_good
				}
				random_list = {

				trigger = {
					is_female = yes
					has_trait = beauty_good
				}
				random_list = {
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_agot_the_fair }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_agot_pretty } #pretty pia :)
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_agot_the_beautiful }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_agot_the_beauty }

					1 = { give_nickname = nick_agot_easy_eyes }

				}

			50 = { #Giant Nicknames
				trigger = {
					NOT = {
						has_trait = dwarf
					}
					OR = {
						has_trait = strong
						has_trait = giant
					}
					has_trait = physique_good

				random_list = {
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_agot_the_mountain }

						give_nickname = nick_agot_the_grumkin_hunter
					}
					1 = {
						trigger = {
							OR = {
								has_trait = arbitrary
								has_trait = arrogant
							}
						}
						give_nickname = nick_agot_wallpisser
					}
					1 = {
						trigger = {
							has_trait = lustful
						}
						give_nickname = nick_agot_the_molestown_guest
					}
				}
			}
			50 = { #Kingsguard Unique Nicknames
				trigger = {
					has_trait = kingsguard
				}
				random_list = {
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_agot_the_white_kingsguard }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_agot_the_pale }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_agot_the_alabaster }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_agot_milkglass }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_agot_the_ivory }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_agot_whiteshield }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_agot_whiteblood }
					1 = {
						trigger = {
							is_agot_knight_trigger = yes
							prowess >= 25
						}
						give_nickname = nick_agot_the_white_knight
					}
					1 = {
						trigger = {
							intrigue >= 12
						}
						give_nickname = nick_agot_the_white_shadow
					}
					1 = {
						trigger = {
							AND = {
								has_trait = strong
								has_trait = physique_good
							}
						}
						give_nickname = nick_agot_the_white_bull
					}
					1 = {
						trigger = {
							culture = culture:northman
						}
						give_nickname = nick_agot_the_snowman
					}
					1 = {
						trigger = {
							OR = {
								has_trait = bastard
								has_trait = legitimized_bastard
							}
						}
						give_nickname = nick_agot_the_white_bastard
					}
					1 = {
						trigger = {
							has_trait = craven
							prowess <= 15
						}
						give_nickname = nick_agot_the_white_worm
					}
					1 = {
						trigger = {
							has_trait = drunkard
						}
						give_nickname = nick_agot_the_white_wine
					}
					1 = {
						trigger = {
							NOR = {
								has_trait = education_martial_prowess_5
								has_trait = education_martial_prowess_4
								has_trait = education_martial_prowess_3
							}
							prowess <= 15
						}
						give_nickname = nick_agot_wastecloak
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

#Bat - Whent/Lothston
agot_nicknames.0025 = {
	type = character_event
	hidden = yes

	trigger = {
		has_any_nickname = no
		OR = {
			dynasty ?= dynasty:dynn_Whent
			dynasty ?= dynasty:dynn_Lothston
			dynasty ?= dynasty:dynn_Cave
		}
	}

	option = {
		random_list = {
			1 = {} #Fallback
			5 = {
				trigger = { black_nickname_trigger = yes NOT = { is_target_in_global_variable_list = { name = assigned_nicknames target = flag:the_black_bat } } }
				modifier = {
					has_trait = nightswatch
					factor = 5
				}
				give_nickname = nick_agot_the_black_bat
				add_to_global_variable_list = {
					name = assigned_nicknames
					target = flag:the_black_bat
					years = 100
				}

			}
			5 = {
				trigger = { white_nickname_trigger = yes NOT = { is_target_in_global_variable_list = { name = assigned_nicknames target = flag:the_white_bat } } }

#####################################

#Birthplace Based Surnames/Nicknames
agot_nicknames.0500 = {
	type = character_event
	hidden = yes

	#Makes them important
	trigger = {
		is_human = yes
		is_adult = yes
		is_lowborn = yes
		exists = root.var:agot_birthplace
		exists = root.location
		NOT = { root.var:agot_birthplace = root.location }
		NOT = { has_character_flag = birthplace_surname }

		NOR = {
			has_trait = bastard
			has_inactive_trait = surname_flowers
			has_inactive_trait = surname_hill
			has_inactive_trait = surname_pyke
			has_inactive_trait = surname_rivers
			has_inactive_trait = surname_sand
			has_inactive_trait = surname_snow
			has_inactive_trait = surname_stone
			has_inactive_trait = surname_storm
			has_inactive_trait = surname_waters
			has_trait = silent_sister
			has_trait = maester
			has_trait = maester_historical
			has_council_position = kingsguard_lord_commander
			any_spouse = { is_ruler = yes }
			is_ruler = yes
		}

		OR = {
			prestige >= 500
			AND = {
				OR = {
					has_trait = nightswatch
					has_trait = kingsguard
				}
				OR = {
					has_trait = education_martial_prowess_3
					has_trait = education_martial_prowess_4
					has_trait = education_martial_prowess_5
					root.prowess >= 20
					root.martial >= 20
				}
			}
			has_trait = education_martial_prowess_4
			has_trait = education_martial_prowess_5
			root.prowess >= 25
			root.diplomacy >= 25
			root.martial >= 25
			root.stewardship >= 25
			root.intrigue >= 25
			root.learning >= 25
		}
	}
	immediate = {
		add_character_flag = birthplace_surname
	}
}

################################################################
### Custom House Nicknames
################################################################

agot_nicknames.9000 = {
	theme = court
	desc = agot_nicknames.9000_desc
	title = agot_nicknames.9000.t

	left_portrait = {
		character = root
		animation = thinking
	}

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			create_character = {
				template = agot_hedgeknight_character
				save_scope_as = dynastic_maester
				location = root.location
			}
		}
	}

	widgets = {
		widget = {
			gui = "agot_custom_dynastic_nickname_widget"
			container = "dynamic_birth_name"
			controller = {
				type = text
				data = {
					key = dynastic_nickname
					default = {
						localization_key = Dynasty_Nickname_Text
					}
				}
			}
			setup_scope = { scope:dynastic_maester = { save_scope_as = text_target } }
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = agot_nicknames.9000.a

		root.dynasty ?= {
			add_dynasty_modifier = unique_dynasty_nickname_modifier
		}

		#Save the word on the maester
		scope:dynastic_maester = {
			set_variable = {
				name = dynastic_nickname
				value = flag:custom
			}
		}

		#save the maester as a global variable so we can point to his corpse for names
		set_global_variable = {
			name = maester
			value = scope:dynastic_maester
		}
	}

	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			#GET HIM OUTTA HEA
			scope:dynastic_maester = {
				change_first_name = Dynasty_Nickname_Text
				agot_make_unpruneable = yes
				death = {
					death_reason = death_vanished
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
